       Products Highlights (for reference only)

       公司產品（僅供參考）


       ANDROID SMART E-PAYMENT SOLUTIONS

       安卓智能電子支付解決方案
       General features: Powered by Android operating system and PCI PTS certified. Compact, portable, equipped with a large
                   high resolution touch screen and inbuilt camera. Support various kinds of payment options, including
                   bank card payments, Near Field Communication (“NFC”) contactless and QR code payments.
                                    PCI PTS
       一般特點：       以安卓作業系統操作，並獲得        認証。外型小巧，方便手持，具有特大高清觸控屏及內置攝像
                                          NFC
                   頭。支援各種支付方式，包括銀行卡支付、       非觸式及二維碼支付等。

       Products Highlights (for reference only)

       公司產品（僅供參考）


       INTEGRATED ECR SOLUTIONS

       一體化智能解決方案
       General Features: Powered by Android operating system, the all-in-one integrated solution delivers cost efficient and space
                   saving features to merchants. Stylish, large color touch screen, customer-facing display and an inbuilt
                   camera.

       一般特點：       以安卓作業系統操作的一體化解決方案，使商戶更節省成本和空間。外型時尚，擁有特大彩色觸控
                   屏、面向顧客的顯示屏及內置攝像頭。











        E700                               E800


       UNATTENDED SOLUTIONS

       自助服務解決方案
       General features: Ideal for self-service sales points such as railway stations, petrol stations, parking lots and kiosks.
                   Products are certified with PCI PTS and have met required standards for anti-vandalism and
                   waterproofing. Support various kinds of payment options and connectivity options include 3G, 4G, WiFi
                   and Bluetooth.

       ANDROID SMART PAYPHONE & PAYTABLET SOLUTIONS

       安卓智能手機及平板支付解決方案
       General Features: Powered by Android operating system and PCI PTS certified. The M30 and M8 are the first-ever Android
                   smartphone and Android tablet with integrated payment module, which are perfect for retail and
                   hospitality industries. Support various kinds of payment options and allow merchants to browse the
                   web, read emails, check social media, make phone calls, take product pictures or record product videos,
                   etc.
                                    PCI PTS M30  M8
       一般特點：       以安卓作業系統操作，並獲得         認証。   和   是首款搭載集成支付模組的安卓智能手機
                   和安卓平板，適合零售和餐飲業採用。支援各種支付方式，商戶可瀏覽網頁、查閱電郵、查看社交媒
                   體、通話、拍攝產品相片或錄製產品視頻等。

       BOARD OF DIRECTORS

       NIE Guoming Chairman
                                                聶國明主席

       Non-GAAP measures

       Certain non-GAAP (generally accepted accounting principles) measures are
                                                若干非公認會計原則指標乃用於評估本集團的表
       used for assessing the Group’s performance. These non-GAAP measures are
                                                現。但該等非公認會計原則指標並非香港公認會計
       not expressly permitted measures under GAAP in Hong Kong and may not be
                                                原則所明確認可的指標，故未必可與其他公司的同
       comparable to similarly titled measures for other companies. Accordingly, such
                                                類指標作比較，因此，該等非公認會計原則指標不
       non-GAAP measures should not be considered as an alternative to operating
                                                應視作經營收入（作為本集團業務表現指標）的替補
       income as an indicator of the operating performance of the Group or as an
                                                或經營活動現金流量（作為衡量流動資金）的替補。
       alternative to cash flows from operating activities as a measure of liquidity.
                                                提供非公認會計原則指標純綷為加強對本集團現時
       The use of non-GAAP measures is provided solely to enhance the overall
                                                財務表現的整體理解，此外由於本集團以往曾向投
       understanding of the Group current financial performance. Additionally because
                                                資者報告若干採用非公認會計原則計算的業績，因
       the Group has historically reported certain non-GAAP results to investors, the
                                                此本集團認為包括非公認會計原則指標可為本集團
       Group considers the inclusion of non-GAAP measures provides consistency in our
                                                的財務報表提供一致性。
       financial reporting.

                                                十四天發給全體董事。根據公司細則按有關情

       benefits in kind, pension rights and the compensation arrangements
                                                會議及對董事會作出建議。人力資源部門負責
       relating to their termination and dismissal. The human resources

       department is responsible for collection and administration of the

       SOGO provides that, in a contract for the sale of goods by description,
                                                《貨品售賣條例》規定，憑貨品說明售貨的合
       there is an implied condition that the goods shall correspond with the

       description. It also provides that where a seller sells goods in the course
                                                它亦規定，凡賣方在業務運作中售貨，有一項
       of a business, there is an implied condition that the goods supplied

                                                質，除非滿足例外條件。
       exception condition is met.
       SOSO regulates the supply of services by the Group in Hong Kong.
                                                《服務提供（隱含條款）條例》規管本集團於香港
       SOSO provides that in a contract for the supply of service where the
                                                的服務提供。《服務提供（隱含條款）條例》規定，
       supplier is acting in the course of a business, there is an implied term
                                                凡提供人是在業務過程中行事，則在有關的服
       that the supplier will carry out the service with reasonable care and
                                                務提供合約中，即有一隱含條款，規定該人須以
       skill. It also provides that under a contract for the supply of a service
                                                合理程度的謹慎及技術作出服務。它亦規定，凡
       where the supplier is acting in the course of a business, if the time
                                                服務提供合約就提供人在業務過程中所提供的
       for carrying out the service is not fixed by the contract or is not left
                                                服務，沒有訂明作出服務的時間，或非以雙方的
       to be determined by the course of dealing between the parties, there
                                                交易過程來決定，則在該合約中即有一隱含條
       is an implied term that the supplier will carry out the service within a

       1  GENERAL INFORMATION                   1
                                                   一般資料
          PAX Global Technology Limited (the “Company”) is an investment
                                                   百富環球科技有限公司（「本公司」）為一
          holding company and together with its subsidiaries (collectively
                                                   間投資控股公司，連同其附屬公司（統稱
          referred to as the “Group”) are principally engaged in the
                                                   「本集團」）主要從事開發及銷售電子支
          development and sales of electronic funds transfer point-of-sale
                                                   付銷售點（「電子支付終端」）產品、提供維
          (“E-payment Terminals”) products, provision of maintenance and
                                                   護及安裝及支付解決方案服務（統稱「電
          installation and payment solution services (collectively, referred to
                                                   子支付終端解決方案業務」）。
          as the “E-payment Terminals solutions business”).
          The Company is a limited liability company incorporated in
                                                   本公司為一間在百慕達註冊成立的有
          Bermuda. The address of its registered office is Clarendon House,
                                                   限責任公司。本公司註冊辦事處的地址
          2 Church Street, Hamilton HM 11, Bermuda.  Clarendon House, 2 Church Street,
                                                   為
                                                   Hamilton HM 11, Bermuda
                                                                   。
          The Company’s shares were listed on the Main Board of The Stock
                                                   本公司的股份於二零一零年十二月二十
          Exchange of Hong Kong Limited (the “Stock Exchange”) on 20
                                                   日在香港聯合交易所有限公司（「聯交
          December 2010.
                                                   所」）主板上市。
          These consolidated financial statements are presented in
                                                   除另有說明外，此綜合財務報表以千港元
          thousands of units of Hong Kong dollars (HK$’000), unless
                                                   （「千港元」）為單位呈列。
          otherwise stated.
       2  SUMMARY  OF SIGNIFICANT ACCOUNTING    2
                                                   主要會計政策概要
          POLICIES
          The principal accounting policies applied in the preparation of
                                                   編製此綜合財務報表所採用的主要會計
          these consolidated financial statements are set out below. These

             of an asset’s fair value less costs of disposal and value in
                                                      處置成本後的價值，與其使用價值
             use. For the purposes of assessing impairment, assets are
                                                      兩者中的較高者。為了評估資產減
             grouped at the lowest levels for which there are separately
                                                      值，本集團按可獨立地確認其現金

             the cash inflows from other assets or groups of assets (cash-
                                                      於其他資產或資產組合的最低層次
             generating units). Non-financial assets other than goodwill

             that suffered an impairment are reviewed for possible

          2.21 Provisions                          2.21
                                                      撥備
             Provisions are recognised when the Group has a present
                                                      當本集團因過往事件承擔現有法
             legal or constructive obligation as a result of past events,
                                                      律或推定性責任，而履行責任有可
             it is probable that an outflow of resources will be required
                                                      能導致資源的流出，且金額能夠可
             to settle the obligation and the amount has been reliably
                                                      靠地估算的情況下，撥備便會被確
             estimated. Provisions are not recognised for future operating
                                                      認。未來經營虧損不會被確認為撥
             losses.
                                                      備。
             Where there are a number of similar obligations, the
                                                      倘承擔若干類似責任，於釐定履行
             likelihood that an outflow will be required in settlement
                                                      責任導致資源流出的可能性時，將
             is determined by considering the class of obligations as a
                                                      以整類責任類別作為整體予以考
             whole. A provision is recognised even if the likelihood of an
                                                      慮。即使同類責任當中任何一項導
             outflow with respect to any one item included in the same
                                                      致資源流出的可能性甚低，撥備亦
             class of obligations may be small.
                                                      會被確認。
             Provisions are measured at the present value of
                                                      撥備以管理層於報告期末為履行現
             management’s best estimate of the expenditures required
                                                      有責任所需支出的最佳估算現值計
             to settle the present obligation at the end of the reporting
                                                      量。計算此等現值使用的貼現率為
             period. The discount rate used to determine the present
                                                      能夠反映當前市場的貨幣時間價值
             value is a pre-tax rate that reflects current market
                                                      及該負債特有風險的稅前貼現率。
             assessments of the time value of money and the risks
                                                      時間流逝導致撥備金額的增幅，會
             specific to the liability. The increase in the provision due to
                                                      被確認為利息開支。
             the passage of time is recognised as interest expense.

          2.24 Leases (as lessee)                  2.24
                                                      租賃（作為承租人）
             Leases are recognised as a right-of-use asset and a
                                                      於租賃資產可供本集團使用的日
             corresponding liability at the date at which the leased asset
                                                      期，本集團會就租賃確認使用權資
             is available for use by the Group.
                                                      產及相應負債。
             Contracts may contain both lease and non-lease
                                                      合同可能同時包含租賃和非租賃組
             components. The Group allocates the consideration in the
                                                      成部分。本集團根據相對獨立價格將
             contract to the lease and non-lease components based on
                                                      合同中的對價分配為租賃和非租賃
             their relative stand-alone prices.
                                                      組成部分。
             Assets and liabilities arising from a lease are initially
                                                      租賃產生的資產及負債初步以現值
             measured on a present value basis. Lease liabilities include
                                                      進行計量。租賃負債包括固定租賃
             the net present value of the fixed lease payments. Lease
                                                      付款的淨現值。根據合理地確定會
             payments to be made under reasonably certain extension
                                                      行使延續選擇權的租賃的租金亦會
             options are also included in the measurement of the liability.
                                                      計入負債計量之內。
             The lease payments are discounted using the interest
                                                      租賃付款採用租賃所隱含的利率予
             rate implicit in the lease. If that rate cannot be readily
                                                      以貼現。倘無法輕易地釐定該利率
             determined, which is generally the case for leases in the
                                                      （為本集團租賃的一般情況），則使
             Group, the lessee’s incremental borrowing rate is used,
                                                      用承租人的增量借貸利率，即個別
             being the rate that the individual lessee would have to
                                                      承租人在類似經濟環境中按類似條
             pay to borrow the funds necessary to obtain an asset of
                                                      款、抵押及條件借入獲得與使用權
             similar value to the right-of-use asset in a similar economic
                                                      資產具有類似價值的資產所需的資
             environment with similar terms, security and conditions.
                                                      金而必須支付的利率。
             To determine the incremental borrowing rate, the Group,
                                                      為釐定增量借款利率，本集團在可
             where possible, uses recent third-party financing received by
                                                      能情況下，使用個別承租人最近獲
             the individual lessee as a starting point, adjusted to reflect
                                                      得的第三方融資為出發點並作出調
             changes in financing conditions since third party financing
                                                      整，以反映自獲得第三方融資以來
             was received and makes adjustments specific to the lease,
                                                      融資條件的變動，及進行特定於租
             e.g. term, country, currency and security.
                                                      賃的相關調整，例如期限、國家、貨
                                                      幣及抵押。
             Lease payments are allocated between principal and finance
                                                      租賃付款會於本金及財務費用之間
             cost. The finance cost is charged to the consolidated income
                                                      作出分配。財務費用會在租賃期間
             statement over the lease period so as to produce a constant
                                                      於綜合收益表扣除，藉以令各期間
             periodic rate of interest on the remaining balance of the
                                                      的負債餘額的週期利率保持一致。
             liability for each period.

          3.2 Capital management                   3.2
                                                      資本管理
             The Group regards its shareholders’ equity as capital. The
                                                      本集團將其股東權益視為資本。本
             Group’s objectives when managing capital are to safeguard
                                                      集團管理資本的目的為保障本集團
             the Group’s ability to continue as a going concern in order
                                                      能繼續以持續經營方式為股東提供
             to provide returns for shareholders and benefits for other
                                                      回報以及為其他利益相關者帶來利
             stakeholders and to maintain an optimal capital structure to
                                                      益，並且維持最佳資本結構以減少
             reduce the cost of capital.
                                                      資本成本。
             In order to maintain or adjust the capital structure, the
                                                      為維持或調整資本結構，本集團可
             Group may adjust the amount of dividends paid to
                                                      調整向股東支付股息的金額、將資
             shareholders, return capital to shareholders, issue new
                                                      本退還予股東、發行新股份、回購
             shares, repurchase the Company’s shares or sell assets to
                                                      本公司股份或出售資產以減少債
             reduce debt.
                                                      務。
             The Group monitors capital on the basis of gearing ratio.
                                                      本集團基於資本負債比率監控資
             This ratio is calculated as total debt divided by total capital.
                                                      本。該比率按債務總額除以資本總
             Total debt includes borrowings of the Group. Total capital is
                                                      額計算。債務總額包括本集團的借
             calculated as equity as shown in the consolidated balance
                                                      貸。資本總額為列於綜合資產負債
             sheet plus total debt.
                                                      表的權益加上債務總額計算。
             The Group did not have any borrowings as at 31 December
                                                      本集團於二零二二年十二月三十一
             2022 and the gearing ratio is not applicable (2021: same).
                                                      日並無借貸，資本負債比率不適用
                                                      （二零二一年：同上）。

             The cost of the land use rights represents the upfront

                                                      物業、工廠及倉庫的租賃合約期限

             negotiated on an individual basis and contain a wide range

             not impose any covenants other than the security interests

             in the leased assets that are held by the lessor. Leased assets
                                                      何契諾。租賃資產不得用作借貸的
             may not be used as security for borrowing purposes.
                                                      擔保。
